<script>
  import Icon from "mdi-svelte";
  import { mdiAccount } from "@mdi/js";
  import { getContext } from "svelte";
  import {
    OIDC_CONTEXT_CLIENT_PROMISE,
    OIDC_CONTEXT_REDIRECT_URI,
    login,
  } from "./OidcContext.svelte";
  const oidcPromise = getContext(OIDC_CONTEXT_CLIENT_PROMISE);
  export let callback_url = getContext(OIDC_CONTEXT_REDIRECT_URI);
  export let preserveRoute;
  export let link = false;
</script>

{#if link}
  <a
    href="#"
    on:click|preventDefault={() =>
      login(oidcPromise, preserveRoute, callback_url)}><slot /></a
  >
{:else}
  <div
    style="display: inline-block; background: #ffffff; border-radius: 120px;"
  >
    <Icon color="#3b5bcb" path={mdiAccount} size="2" />
  </div>
  <button
    class="button login"
    on:click|preventDefault={() =>
      login(oidcPromise, preserveRoute, callback_url)}><slot /></button
  >
{/if}

<style>
  .login {
    border: none;
    outline: none;
    background: transparent;
    font-family: "Inter";
  }
  .login:hover {
    color: #3b5bcb;
